filter the results based on some criteria.\n6: // \t Bootstrap: Create the plugins found in the discovery stage and enrich them with metadata.\n7: // \t Validation: Validate the plugins based on some verification system is implemented across multiple files that work together to ensure plugin integrity and security. Here is the comprehensive implementation:\\n\\n## Signature Manifest and Calculation\\n\\nThe core signature verification logic resides in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/manifest.go`. The `Signature` struct implements the `SignatureCalculator` interface and provides the `Calculate()` method which orchestrates the entire verification process. This method:\\n1. Checks for a default signature from the plugin source\\n2. Reads the plugin manifest from the filesystem using `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`\\n3. Handles unsigned plugins appropriately\\n4. Validates manifest structure via `validateManifest()`\\n5. Verifies file hashes via `verifyHash()`\\n6. Returns a `Signature` struct with the verification result\\n\\nThe `readPluginManifest()` method decodes PGP-signed manifest files and parses the JSON content. The `validateManifest()` method checks required manifest fields and calls `Verify()` to validate the cryptographic signature using OpenPGP.\\n\\n## Signature Validation\\n\\nSignature validation happens in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` through the `Validation` struct implementing the `Validator` interface. The `ValidateSignature()` method:\\n1. Checks if the signature is already valid or internal (core plugin)\\n2. Handles nested plugins by inheriting parent signature\\n3. Enforces signature requirements based on signature status\\n4. Allows unsigned plugins only if authorized via `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`\\n5. Returns errors for invalid or modified signatures\\n\\n## Unsigned Plugin Authorization\\n\\nThe `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/authorizer.go` file contains the `UnsignedPluginAuthorizer` struct implementing `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`. The `CanLoadPlugin()` method allows unsigned plugins if:\\n1. They have a valid signature (always permitted)\\n2. Grafana is running in development mode\\n3. The plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n\\nThis allowlist enforcement prevents unauthorized unsigned plugins while providing a security override mechanism.\\n\\n## Public Key Management\\n\\nPlugin signatures are verified using PGP public keys managed through two systems:\\n\\n**Static Key Retriever** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key for verifying officially signed plugins. The `KeyRetriever` implements the retrieval interface.\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retriever** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the Grafana.com API. The `KeyRetriever` struct:\\n1. Downloads keys via `downloadKeys()` from `GrafanaComAPIURL/plugins/ci/keys`\\n2. Caches keys in the `KeyStore` with configurable sync intervals (10 days)\\n3. Implements `GetPublicKey()` to retrieve keys for manifest verification\\n4. Supports force-refresh via `PluginForcePublicKeyDownload` configuration\\n\\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keystore/keystore.go` provides the `KeyStore` service for persistent caching of public keys using the KVStore infrastructure.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature verification is integrated into the plugin loading pipeline at multiple stages:\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): The `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` method calls the signature calculator's `Calculate()` method to determine each plugin's signature status before plugin object creation.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): The `PluginSignatureValidator` validates signatures via `SignatureValidationStep()`. The `DefaultValidateFuncs()` includes signature validation as a core validation function.\\n\\n**Services Integration** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): The `SignatureValidation` struct validates signatures at the services layer, recording errors with the error tracker for disabled plugins.\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is configured via:\\n- `pkg/plugins/config/config.go`: `PluginManagementCfg` struct containing `PluginsAllowUnsigned []string`\\n- `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go`: The `readPluginSettings()` function reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` from INI configuration\\n\\nThis allows administrators to explicitly permit specific unsigned plugins in production while maintaining security by default.\\n\\n## Signature Status Types\\n\\n`pkg/plugins/models.go` defines the signature states:\\n- `SignatureStatusInternal`: Core plugins bundled with Grafana\\n- `SignatureStatusValid`: Successfully verified plugins\\n- `SignatureStatusInvalid`: Failed signature verification\\n- `SignatureStatusModified`: Valid signature but content mismatch\\n- `SignatureStatusUnsigned`: Missing manifest file\\n\\nCorresponding error codes (`ErrorCodeSignatureMissing`, `ErrorCodeSignatureInvalid`, `ErrorCodeSignatureModified`) track signature-related failures for disabled plugin tracking.\\n\\n## Interfaces\\n\\nThe system uses dependency injection with interfaces defined in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\\n- `Validator`: Validates plugin signatures\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Persists cached public keys\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes loading unsigned plugins\\n\\n## Wire Checks for a default signature from the plugin source\\n2. Reads the plugin manifest from the filesystem using `ReadPluginManifestFromFS()`\\n3. Handles unsigned plugins appropriately\\n4. Returns a `Signature` struct with the verification result\\n\\nThe `readPluginManifest()` method decodes PGP-signed manifest files and parses the JSON content. The `validateManifest()` method checks required manifest fields and calls `Verify()` to validate the cryptographic signature using OpenPGP.\\n\\n## Signature Validation\\n\\nSignature validation happens in `pkg/plugins/manager/signature/signature.go` through the `Validation` struct implementing the `Validator` interface. The `ValidateSignature()` method:\\n1. Checks if the signature is already valid or internal (core plugin)\\n2. Handles nested plugins by inheriting parent signature\\n3. The plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n\\nThis allowlist enforcement prevents unauthorized unsigned plugins while providing a security override mechanism.\\n\\n## Public Key Management\\n\\nPlugin signatures are verified using PGP public keys managed through two systems:\\n\\n**Static Key Retriever** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key for verifying officially signed plugins. The `KeyRetriever` implements the retrieval interface.\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retriever** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the Grafana.com API. The `KeyRetriever` struct:\\n1. Downloads keys via `downloadKeys()` from `GrafanaComAPIURL/plugins/ci/keys`\\n2. Caches keys in the `KeyStore` with configurable sync intervals (10 days)\\n3. Implements `GetPublicKey()` to retrieve keys for manifest verification\\n4. Supports force-refresh via `PluginForcePublicKeyDownload` configuration\\n\\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keystore/keystore.go` provides the `KeyStore` service for persistent caching of public keys using the KVStore infrastructure.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature verification is integrated into the plugin loading pipeline at multiple stages:\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): The `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` method calls the signature calculator's `Calculate()` method to determine each plugin's signature status before plugin object creation.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): The `PluginSignatureValidator` validates signatures via `SignatureValidationStep()`. The `DefaultValidateFuncs()` includes signature validation as a core validation function.\\n\\n**Services Integration** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): The `SignatureValidation` struct validates signatures at the services layer, recording errors with the error tracker for disabled plugins.\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is configured via:\\n- `pkg/plugins/config/config.go`: `PluginManagementCfg` struct containing `PluginsAllowUnsigned []string`\\n- `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go`: The `readPluginSettings()` function reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` from INI configuration\\n\\nThis allows administrators to explicitly permit specific unsigned plugins in production while maintaining security by default.\\n\\n## Signature Status Types\\n\\n`pkg/plugins/models.go` defines the signature states:\\n- `SignatureStatusInternal`: Core plugins bundled with Grafana\\n- `SignatureStatusValid`: Successfully verified plugins\\n- `SignatureStatusInvalid`: Failed signature verification\\n- `SignatureStatusModified`: Valid signature but content mismatch\\n- `SignatureStatusUnsigned`: Missing manifest file\\n\\nCorresponding error codes (`ErrorCodeSignatureMissing`, `ErrorCodeSignatureInvalid`, `ErrorCodeSignatureModified`) track signature-related failures for disabled plugin tracking.\\n\\n## signatures\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Persists cached public keys\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes loading unsigned plugins\\n\\n## Wire The plugin ID is in the `PluginsAllowUnsigned` configuration list\\n\\nThis allowlist enforcement prevents unauthorized unsigned plugins while providing a security override mechanism.\\n\\n## Public Key Management\\n\\nPlugin signatures are verified using PGP public keys managed through two systems:\\n\\n**Static Key Retriever** (`pkg/plugins/manager/signature/statickey/static_retriever.go`): Provides a hardcoded Grafana Labs public key for verifying officially signed plugins. The `KeyRetriever` implements the retrieval interface.\\n\\n**Dynamic Key Retriever** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keyretriever/dynamic/dynamic_retriever.go`): Downloads and caches public keys from the Grafana.com API. The `KeyRetriever` struct:\\n1. Downloads keys via `downloadKeys()` from `GrafanaComAPIURL/plugins/ci/keys`\\n2. Caches keys in the `KeyStore` with configurable sync intervals (10 days)\\n3. Implements `GetPublicKey()` to retrieve keys for manifest verification\\n4. Supports force-refresh via `PluginForcePublicKeyDownload` configuration\\n\\nThe `pkg/services/pluginsintegration/keystore/keystore.go` provides the `KeyStore` service for persistent caching of public keys using the KVStore infrastructure.\\n\\n## Plugin Loading Pipeline\\n\\nSignature verification is integrated into the plugin loading pipeline at multiple stages:\\n\\n**Bootstrap Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/bootstrap/steps.go`): The `DefaultConstructor.Construct()` method calls the signature calculator's `Calculate()` method to determine each plugin's signature status before plugin object creation.\\n\\n**Validation Stage** (`pkg/plugins/manager/pipeline/validation/steps.go`): The `PluginSignatureValidator` validates signatures via `SignatureValidationStep()`. The `DefaultValidateFuncs()` includes signature validation as a core validation function.\\n\\n**Services Integration** (`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pipeline/steps.go`): The `SignatureValidation` struct validates signatures at the services layer, recording errors with the error tracker for disabled plugins.\\n\\n## Configuration\\n\\nThe unsigned plugin allowlist is configured via:\\n- `pkg/plugins/config/config.go`: `PluginManagementCfg` struct containing `PluginsAllowUnsigned []string`\\n- `pkg/setting/setting_plugins.go`: The `readPluginSettings()` function reads `allow_loading_unsigned_plugins` from INI configuration\\n\\nThis allows administrators to explicitly permit specific unsigned plugins in production while maintaining security by default.\\n\\n## Signature Status Types\\n\\n`pkg/plugins/models.go` defines the signature states:\\n- `SignatureStatusInternal`: Core plugins bundled with Grafana\\n- `SignatureStatusValid`: Successfully verified plugins\\n- `SignatureStatusInvalid`: Failed signature verification\\n- `SignatureStatusModified`: Valid signature but content mismatch\\n- `SignatureStatusUnsigned`: Missing manifest file\\n\\nCorresponding error codes (`ErrorCodeSignatureMissing`, `ErrorCodeSignatureInvalid`, `ErrorCodeSignatureModified`) track signature-related failures for disabled plugin tracking.\\n\\n## Interfaces\\n\\nThe system uses dependency injection with interfaces defined in `pkg/plugins/ifaces.go`:\\n- `SignatureCalculator`: Calculates plugin signature state\\n- `Validator`: Validates plugin signatures\\n- `KeyRetriever`: Retrieves public keys for verification\\n- `KeyStore`: Persists cached public keys\\n- `PluginLoaderAuthorizer`: Authorizes loading unsigned plugins\\n\\n## Wire Integration\\n\\n`pkg/services/pluginsintegration/pluginsintegration.go` wires all components together using dependency injection, binding implementations to interfaces and configuring the validation pipeline with signature validation steps.\\n\\nThis multi-layered architecture ensures plugin integrity through cryptographic verification while allowing administrative overrides for specific use
